  <script>
var icookiecolor=$.cookie("icookiecolor");
if(typeof (icookiecolor) != "undefined")
{
	if(icookiecolor==2)
	{
	    $(".news_info").attr("class","news_info news_gry");	
		$("#i_colorset").attr("onclick","setlistcolor(1)"); 
		$("#i_colorset").text("蓝色");
    }
}
function setlistcolor(ivalue)
{
	if(ivalue==1)
	{
		$(".news_info").attr("class","news_info news_blue");	
		$("#i_colorset").attr("onclick","setlistcolor(2)"); 
		$("#i_colorset").text("灰色");
	}else{
	    $(".news_info").attr("class","news_info news_gry");	
		$("#i_colorset").attr("onclick","setlistcolor(1)"); 
		$("#i_colorset").text("蓝色");
	}
	$.cookie("icookiecolor",ivalue,{expires: 3650, path: '/',domain:'mydrivers.com'})
}
function setbodyfont(ivalue)
{
	$("#i_font1,#i_font2,#i_font3").css('font-weight','normal'); 
	$("#i_font1,#i_font2,#i_font3").css('text-decoration','none'); 
	$("#i_font"+ivalue).css('font-weight','bold'); 
	$("#i_font"+ivalue).css('text-decoration','underline'); 
	if(ivalue==1)
	{
		$("body").attr("class","body_yahei");
	}else if(ivalue==2){
	   $("body").attr("class","body_songti");	
	}else
	{
		$("body").attr("class","body_heiti");	
	}
	$.cookie("icookiefont",ivalue,{expires: 3650, path: '/',domain:'mydrivers.com'})
}
function i_showset()
{
	$(".edit_s").show();
	$("#i_symn").attr("class","menu");
	$("#ishowset").attr("class","edit_img_cur");
}
$(function(){ 
	$(document).bind("click",function(e){ 
	var target = $(e.target); 
	if(target.closest(".edit_s").length == 0){ 
	$(".edit_s").hide(); 
	$("#i_symn").attr("class","nav_hover");
	$("#ishowset").attr("class","edit_img");} 
	}) 

$(".edit_s").hover(function(){},function(){ 
        $(this).hide();
	    $("#i_symn").attr("class", "nav_hover");
	    $("#ishowset").attr("class", "edit_img");
	})
}) 
</script>
